msg:Great location, friendly front desk staff and we even got a free upgrade on our room. The room was lovely, nice and big with good facilities and a wonderful deep bath.

The pool is lovely and big with lots of seats and tables around. Unfortunately there was only 1 solitary sunlounger so it wasn't set up for sunbathing. A real shame as it was a great area, nicely decorated. There were also free coffee, soft drinks and beers from the lobby cafe area which could be taken outside (though some staff didn't seem to know about this). Not the best for families, much better equipt for adults. 

The food for breakfast was OK, not much choice and things often ran out. There is a station for freshly cooked eggs but the staff seemed unwilling to cook me fresh eggs when they had ones sat on the hotplate already. This was a letdown as the dining area is nice and could be a lovely experience if the food and dining room staff were better. We didn't pay extra for breakfast so weren't too annoyed but I would not have paid extra for the experience.

Overall I would definitely stay again if the price were reasonable!

It's the farthest place from the airport. It only takes 20 minutes to take a taxi to the airport. Parking is available underground, and parking is free if you register your car number.
